33rd - 64th Decklists
=====================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX GUANGZHOU 2016](/en/events/coverage/gpgua16)
 on August 28, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/chapman.jpg)
By Chapman Sim











We posted [9th - 32nd decklists here](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpgua16/9th-32nd-decklists-2016-08-28), but we know that you want even more! Because we love you so very much, here are all the decklists of all cashing participants!


Have fun poring over the pages!


*(\*Special thanks to the helpful Tournament Organizer, Panda Events, for helping out with 16 decklists!)*
